üåø Contact with nature is the best early education~üë®üë©üëß

üåøThis stop, we came to Shanghai Songjiang Guangfulin.

üìçLocation:
The suburbs of Shanghai are always closer than Shanghai~ Suitable for young babies, or parents who have not taken their babies far away~ From near to far, try the water first to see if your baby can adapt to the journeyüöó
